<script>
function defineDeviceOrientation() {
    var screenRatio;
    if (screen && screen.height > 0 && screen.width > 0) {
        screenRatio = screen.width / screen.height;
    } else if (window.innerHeight != 0) {
        screenRatio = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
    }

    if (screenRatio) {
        if (screenRatio >= 1) {
            return 'landscape';
        } else {
            return 'portrait';
        }
    }
}
